# Technical Documentation

## Project Overview

A symbolic AI-powered assistant designed to help tenants and legal professionals analyze and challenge default judgments in unlawful detainer (eviction) cases under California Code of Civil Procedure Â§ 473.5.

## File Details

### ğŸ“„ streamlit_app.py

**Imports:**
- `import streamlit as st`
- `from openai import OpenAI`
- `import yaml`
- `from typing import Dict`
- `from typing import Any`
- `from typing import List`
- `from legal_logic_aligned import evaluate_rules`
- `from response_logic import explain_output`
- `from summary_generator import generate_summary`
- `from summary_generator import save_summary`
- `from motion_drafter import render_motion_template`
- `from datetime import datetime`

**Functions:**
- `get_openai_client(api_key)`
  - **Description:** Initialize and cache the OpenAI client.
  - **Parameters:**
    - `api_key: str`
  - **Returns:** `OpenAI`
- `cached_evaluate_rules(facts)`
  - **Description:** Cache the legal evaluation results.
  - **Parameters:**
    - `facts`
  - **Returns:** `Dict[str, Any]`
- `cached_explain_output(result)`
  - **Description:** Cache the GPT explanation.
  - **Parameters:**
    - `result`
  - **Returns:** `str`
- `load_questions()`
  - **Description:** Load and cache intake questions.
  - **Returns:** `List[Dict[str, Any]]`
- `generate_motion(facts, result, explanation)`
  - **Description:** Generate motion text and handle errors
  - **Parameters:**

### ğŸ“„ code-quality-checker-streamlit.py

**Description:**
Streamlit Static Analysis Tool

This script runs multiple static analysis tools on a Streamlit project and generates
a consolidated summary report without making any changes to the codebase.

Tools used:
- pylint: Detects misuse of widgets, naming issues, improper conditionals
- mypy: Ensures Streamlit inputs are properly typed
- bandit: Warns about unsafe use of secrets and security issues
- vulture: Finds unused UI elements or logic blocks
- flake8: Helps with code style readability

**Imports:**
- `import os`
- `import sys`
- `import subprocess`
- `import argparse`
- `import json`
- `from datetime import datetime`
- `from typing import Dict`
- `from typing import List`
- `from typing import Any`
- `from typing import Tuple`

**Functions:**
- `parse_pylint(output)`
  - **Description:** Parse pylint JSON output
  - **Parameters:**
    - `output: str`
  - **Returns:** `List[Dict[str, Any]]`
- `parse_mypy(output)`
  - **Description:** Parse mypy JSON output
  - **Parameters:**
    - `output: str`
  - **Returns:** `List[Dict[str, Any]]`
- `parse_bandit(output)`
  - **Description:** Parse bandit JSON output
  - **Parameters:**
    - `output: str`
  - **Returns:** `List[Dict[str, Any]]`
- `parse_flake8(output)`
  - **Description:** Parse flake8 JSON output
  - **Parameters:**
    - `output: str`
  - **Returns:** `List[Dict[str, Any]]`
- `parse_vulture(output)`
  - **Description:** Parse vulture text output
  - **Parameters:**
    - `output: str`
  - **Returns:** `List[Dict[str, Any]]`
- `run_tool(tool_name, target_path)`
  - **Description:** Run a tool and return parsed results and success status
  - **Parameters:**
    - `tool_name: str`
    - `target_path: str`
  - **Returns:** `Tuple[List[Dict[str, Any]], bool]`
- `is_streamlit_related(issue)`
  - **Description:** Check if an issue is Streamlit-related based on keywords
  - **Parameters:**
    - `issue`
  - **Returns:** `bool`
- `generate_summary(results)`
  - **Description:** Generate a summary report from all tool results
  - **Parameters:**
    - `results`
  - **Returns:** `str`
- `save_report(report, output_path)`
  - **Description:** Save the report to a file
  - **Parameters:**
    - `report: str`
    - `output_path: str`
  - **Returns:** `None`
- `main()`
  - **Description:** Main function to run the tools and generate the report

**Key Variables:**

### ğŸ“„ streamlit-doc-generator.py

**Description:**
Streamlit Project Documentation Generator

This script analyzes a Streamlit project's structure and code to generate
comprehensive technical documentation in Markdown format.

**Imports:**
- `import os`
- `import ast`
- `import re`
- `import sys`
- `import importlib.util`
- `from collections import defaultdict`
- `from typing import Dict`
- `from typing import List`
- `from typing import Set`
- `from typing import Tuple`
- `from typing import Any`
- `from typing import Optional`
- `import argparse`
- `import logging`
- `import json`

**Classes:**
- `class StreamlitComponentExtractor(ast.NodeVisitor)`
  - **Description:** Extract Streamlit components and other relevant information from AST.
  - **Methods:**
    - `__init__(self)`
    - `visit_Import(self, node)`
      - Extract import statements.
    - `visit_ImportFrom(self, node)`
      - Extract from import statements.
    - `visit_Assign(self, node)`
      - Extract variable assignments.
    - `visit_FunctionDef(self, node)`
      - Extract function definitions and docstrings.
    - `visit_ClassDef(self, node)`
      - Extract class definitions and docstrings.
    - `visit_Call(self, node)`
      - Extract function/method calls, focusing on Streamlit components.
- `class DocumentationGenerator`
  - **Description:** Generate Markdown documentation from analyzed project files.
  - **Methods:**
    - `__init__(self, project_path, output_file, ignore_dirs)`
      - Initialize the documentation generator.

Args:
    project_path: Root directory of the Streamlit project
    output_file: Path where the documentation will be written
    ignore_dirs: List of directory names to ignore
    - `_is_ignored(self, path)`
      - Check if a path should be ignored.
    - `_extract_file_info(self, file_path)`
      - Extract information from a file based on its extension.
    - `_extract_python_file_info(self, file_path)`
      - Extract information from a Python file.
    - `_extract_requirements_info(self, file_path)`
      - Extract information from a requirements.txt file.
    - `_extract_readme_info(self, file_path)`
      - Extract information from a README.md file.
    - `collect_project_info(self)`
      - Walk through the project and collect information about all files.
    - `_generate_project_structure_md(self)`
      - Generate Markdown representation of the project structure.
    - `_add_structure(structure, level)`
    - `_generate_python_file_md(self, file_path, file_data)`
      - Generate Markdown documentation for a Python file.
    - `_generate_requirements_md(self)`
      - Generate Markdown documentation for requirements.
    - `_generate_streamlit_components_summary(self)`
      - Generate a summary of all Streamlit components used in the project.
    - `generate_documentation(self)`
      - Generate the full documentation and write it to the output file.

**Functions:**
- `main()`
  - **Description:** Main entry point for the documentation generator.

**Key Variables:**

### ğŸ“„ summary_generator.py

**Description:**
This module generates a professional, plain text case summary that includes:
âœ… User inputs (facts)
âœ… Legal rule result
âœ… GPT-generated explanation
The summary is saved to a file: case-summary.txt
The user can also download it via Streamlit's download button.

ğŸ“Œ Disclaimer: This tool is for research and educational use only. It is not legal advice.

**Imports:**
- `import datetime`
- `from typing import Dict`
- `from typing import Any`
- `from typing import Optional`

**Functions:**
- `generate_summary(facts, result, explanation, case_name)`
  - **Description:** Create a formatted case summary string.

Args:
    facts (dict): Input data from the form (served_date, motion_date, etc.)
    result (dict): Output from evaluate_rules()
    explanation (str): GPT explanation of legal result
    case_name (str): Optional case name or placeholder

Returns:
    str: Formatted summary text
  - **Parameters:**
    - `facts`
    - `result`
    - `explanation`
    - `case_name: str`
  - **Returns:** `str`
- `save_summary(summary, filename)`
  - **Description:** Save the summary text to a local file for backend use.

Args:
    summary (str): Case summary text
    filename (str): Output file name
  - **Parameters:**
    - `summary: str`
    - `filename: str`
  - **Returns:** `None`

**Key Variables:**
